</li><li><b>BWV 767</b> — <a href="/wiki/O_Gott,_du_frommer_Gott,_BWV_767_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="O Gott, du frommer Gott, BWV 767 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Chorale partita on "O Gott, du frommer Gott"</a>
</li><li><b>BWV 768</b> — <a href="/wiki/Sei_gegr%C3%BCsset,_Jesu_g%C3%BCtig,_BWV_768_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Sei gegrüsset, Jesu gütig, BWV 768 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Chorale partita on "Sei gegrüsset, Jesu gütig"</a> 
</li><li><b>BWV 769</b> — <a href="/wiki/Vom_himmel_hoch,_da_komm_ich_her,_BWV_769_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Vom himmel hoch, da komm ich her, BWV 769 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)" class="mw-redirect">Canonic variations on "Vom Himmel hoch, da komm' ich her"</a>
</li><li><b>BWV 770</b> — <a href="/wiki/Ach,_was_soll_ich_S%C3%BCnder_machen,_BWV_770_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Ach, was soll ich Sünder machen, BWV 770 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Chorale variations "Ach, was soll ich Sünder machen" (spurious)</a>
</li><li><b>BWV 771</b> — <a href="/wiki/Allein_Gott_in_der_H%C3%B6h_sei_Ehr_(Vetter,_Nicolaus)" title="Allein Gott in der Höh sei Ehr (Vetter, Nicolaus)">Chorale variations "Allein Gott in der Höh' sei Ehr'" (spurious; now attributed to Nicolaus Vetter)</a>
</li><li><b>BWV 587</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Aria_in_F_major,_BWV_587_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Aria in F major, BWV 587 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)" class="mw-redirect">Aria in F major</a></i> (spurious, after <a href="/wiki/Category:Couperin,_Fran%C3%A7ois" title="Category:Couperin, François">François Couperin</a>)
</li><li><b>BWV 588</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Canzona_in_D_minor,_BWV_588_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Canzona in D minor, BWV 588 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Canzona in D minor</a></i>
</li><li><b>BWV 589</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Alla_breve_in_D_major,_BWV_589_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Alla breve in D major, BWV 589 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Alla breve in D major</a></i>
</li><li><b>BWV 590</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Pastorale_in_F_major,_BWV_590_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Pastorale in F major, BWV 590 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Pastorale in F major</a></i> (incomplete)
</li><li><b>BWV 591</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Kleines_harmonisches_Labyrinth,_BWV_591_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Kleines harmonisches Labyrinth, BWV 591 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Kleines harmonisches Labyrinth</a></i> (doubtful; possibly by <a href="/wiki/Category:Heinichen,_Johann_David" title="Category:Heinichen, Johann David">Johann David Heinichen</a>)
</li><li><b>BWV 598</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Pedal-Exercitium,_BWV_598_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Pedal-Exercitium, BWV 598 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Pedal-Exercitium</a></i> ("Pedal Exercise") (doubtful; possbily by <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Carl_Philipp_Emanuel" title="Category:Bach, Carl Philipp Emanuel">Carl Philipp Emanuel Bach</a>)
</li><li><b>BWV 802-805</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/4_Duettos,_BWV_802-805_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="4 Duettos, BWV 802-805 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">4 Duettos</a></i> (from Clavierübung Volume III)
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
